Each block is 16 bytes\n\n# --- Helper Functions ---\n\ndef get_block_number(sector, block):\n    \"\"\"Calculate absolute block number from sector and block.\"\"\"\n    # Sectors 0-31: 4 blocks/sector, sectors 32+: 16 blocks/sector\n    if sector < 32:\n        return sector * 4 + block\n    else:\n        return 32 * 4 + (sector - 32) * 16 + block\n\ndef send_apdu(connection, apdu, expect_response=True):\n    \"\"\"Send an APDU and return response and status words.\"\"\"\n    response, sw1, sw2 = connection.transmit(apdu)\n    if expect_response:\n        print(f\"APDU: {toHexString(apdu)} -> {toHexString(response)} SW1={hex(sw1)} SW2={hex(sw2)}\")\n    return response, sw1, sw2\n\ndef load_authentication_key(connection, key, key_number=0x00):\n    \"\"\"\n    Load authentication key into reader volatile memory.\n    For ACR readers, use the 'LOAD KEY' APDU.\n    \"\"\"\n    # PCSC: FF 82 00 [key_number] 06 [key bytes]\n    apdu = [0xFF, 0x82, 0x00, key_number, 0x06] + key\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu, expect_response=False)\n\ndef authenticate_block(connection, block_number, key_type=\"A\", key_number=0x00):\n    \"\"\"\n    Authenticate a block for read/write.\n    key_type: \"A\" or \"B\"\n    \"\"\"\n    # PCSC: FF 86 00 00 05 [version=01] [block] [key type] [key number]\n    key_type_code = 0x60 if key_type == \"A\" else 0x61\n    apdu = [\n        0xFF, 0x86, 0x00, 0x00, 0x05,\n        0x01,  # Version\n        0x00,  # Reserved\n        block_number,\n        key_type_code,\n        key_number\n    ]\n    _, sw1, sw2 = send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n    if (sw1, sw2) != (0x90, 0x00):\n        raise Exception(f\"Authentication failed for block {block_number} (SW1={hex(sw1)}, SW2={hex(sw2)})\")\n\ndef read_block(connection, block_number):\n    \"\"\"Read 16 bytes from a block.\"\"\"\n    # PCSC: FF B0 00 [block] 10\n    apdu = [0xFF, 0xB0, 0x00, block_number, 0x10]\n    response, sw1, sw2 = send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n    if (sw1, sw2) == (0x90, 0x00):\n        return response\n    else:\n        raise Exception(f\"Read failed (SW1={hex(sw1)}, SW2={hex(sw2)})\")\n\ndef write_block(connection, block_number, data):\n    \"\"\"Write 16 bytes to a block.\"\"\"\n    if len(data) != 16:\n        raise ValueError(\"Data must be exactly 16 bytes.\")\n    # PCSC: FF D6 00 [block] 10 [data]\n    apdu = [0xFF, 0xD6, 0x00, block_number, 0x10] + data\n    _, sw1, sw2 = send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n    if (sw1, sw2) != (0x90, 0x00):\n        raise Exception(f\"Write failed (SW1={hex(sw1)}, SW2={hex(sw2)})\")\n\ndef personalize_sector_trailer(connection, sector, keyA, access_bits, keyB):\n    \"\"\"\n    Write new keys and access bits to the sector trailer.\n    Sector trailer is always the last block of the sector.\n    \"\"\"\n    if sector < 32:\n        block = sector * 4 + 3\n    else:\n        block = 32 * 4 + (sector - 32) * 16 + 15\n    # Sector trailer structure: KeyA (6 bytes) | Access Bits (4 bytes) | KeyB (6 bytes)\n    trailer = keyA + access_bits + keyB\n    authenticate_block(connection, block, \"A\")  # Use default key A\n    write_block(connection, block, trailer)\n    print(f\"Personalized sector {sector} trailer.\")\n\ndef create_access_bits(c1, c2, c3):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create access bits for sector trailer.\n    c1, c2, c3: 4 lists (one per block), each with 3 bits (C1, C2, C3).\n    Returns 4 bytes.\n    \"\"\"\n    # See NXP MIFARE datasheet for bit layout\n    def pack_bits(bits):\n        return (bits[2] << 2) | (bits[1] << 1) | bits[0]\n    ab0 = (pack_bits(c1[3]) << 4) | pack_bits(c1[2])\n    ab1 = (pack_bits(c1[1]) << 4) | pack_bits(c1[0])\n    ab2 = (pack_bits(c2[3]) << 4) | pack_bits(c2[2])\n    ab3 = (pack_bits(c2[1]) << 4) | pack_bits(c2[0])\n    # For simplicity, use default access bits (all 0: full access)\n    return [0xFF, 0x07, 0x80, 0x69]\n\n# --- Main Script ---\n\ndef main():\n    print(\"MIFARE Plus EV2 Personalization Script\")\n    # 1. List PC/SC readers\n    rlist = readers()\n    if not rlist:\n        print(\"No smart card readers found.\")\n        return\n    print(\"Available readers:\")\n    for i, r in enumerate(rlist):\n        print(f\" [{i}] {r}\")\n    reader = rlist[0]  # Use first reader\n    print(f\"Using reader: {reader}\")\n\n    # 2. Connect to card\n    connection = reader.createConnection()\n    try:\n        connection.connect()\n    except NoCardException:\n        print(\"No card detected. Please insert a MIFARE Plus EV2 card.\")\n        return\n    except CardConnectionException as e:\n        print(f\"Failed to connect to card: {e}\")\n        return\n\n    # 3. Load default key into reader\n    print(\"Loading default key into reader...\")\n    load_authentication_key(connection, DEFAULT_KEY, key_number=0x00)\n\n    # 4. Authenticate to EF sector blocks\n    print(\"Authenticating to EF sector blocks...\")\n    for block in EF_BLOCKS:\n        abs_block = get_block_number(EF_SECTOR, block)\n        authenticate_block(connection, abs_block, \"A\", key_number=0x00)\n\n    # 5. Write sample data to EF blocks\n    print(\"Writing sample data to EF blocks...\")\n    sample_data = [\n        b'EF-Header-Record1',  # Block 0 (16 bytes)\n        b'UserData-Record2!!', # Block 1 (16 bytes)\n        b'UserData-Record3!!'  # Block 2 (16 bytes)\n    ]\n    for i, block in enumerate(EF_BLOCKS):\n        abs_block = get_block_number(EF_SECTOR, block)\n        write_block(connection, abs_block, list(sample_data[i]))\n\n    # 6. Read back and display data\n    print(\"Reading EF blocks:\")\n    for block in EF_BLOCKS:\n        abs_block = get_block_number(EF_SECTOR, block)\n        data = read_block(connection, abs_block)\n        print(f\" Block {abs_block}: {bytes(data).decode(errors='replace')}\")\n\n    # 7. Configure access rights (personalize sector trailer)\n    print(\"Configuring access rights for EF sector...\")\n    # For demonstration, use default access bits (full access)\n    access_bits = [0xFF, 0x07, 0x80, 0x69]\n    personalize_sector_trailer(\n        connection,\n        EF_SECTOR,\n        NEW_KEY_A,\n        access_bits,\n        NEW_KEY_B\n    )\n\n    print(\"Personalization complete.\")\n\n    # 8. Simulate responses based on INS byte\n        ins = apdu[1]\n        if ins == 0xA4:  # SELECT\n            # Always succeed\n            return ([0x90, 0x00], 0x90, 0x00)\n        elif ins == 0x82:  # EXTERNAL AUTH\n            # Succeed if key length is 16\n            if len(apdu) == 5 + 16:\n                return ([0x90, 0x00], 0x90, 0x00)\n            else:\n                return ([], 0x69, 0x82)  # Security status not satisfied\n        elif ins == 0xE0:  # CREATE FILE\n            # Succeed if size is reasonable\n            if apdu[10] <= 128:\n                return ([0x90, 0x00], 0x90, 0x00)\n            else:\n                return ([], 0x6A, 0x84)  # Not enough memory\n        elif ins == 0xD6:  # WRITE BINARY\n            # Succeed if data length is not zero\n            if apdu[4] > 0:\n                return ([0x90, 0x00], 0x90, 0x00)\n            else:\n                return ([], 0x67, 0x00)  # Wrong length\n        elif ins == 0xB0:  # READ BINARY\n            # Return dummy data of requested length\n            length = apdu[4]\n            return ([0xFF] * length, 0x90, 0x00)\n        else:\n            return ([], 0x6D, 0x00)  # INS not supported\n\n    def reset(self):\n        self.transmit_calls.clear()\n\nclass TestMifarePersonalization(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.conn = DummyConnection()\n\n    def test_select_application_success(self):\n        aid = [0xD2, 0x76, 0x00, 0x00, 0x85, 0x01, 0x01]\n        response = select_application(self.conn, aid)\n        self.assertEqual(response, ([0x90, 0x00], 0x90, 0x00))\n        # Too short\n        response = authenticate_ev2(self.conn, key_no, key)\n        self.assertEqual(response, ([], 0x69, 0x82))\n\n    def test_create_ef_file_success(self):\n        ef = EF_FILES[0]\n        response = create_ef_file(self.conn, ef['fid'], ef['size'], ef['read_key'], ef['write_key'])\n        self.assertEqual(response, ([0x90, 0x00], 0x90, 0x00))\n        # Check correct APDU structure\n        apdu = self.conn.transmit_calls[-1]\n        self.assertEqual(apdu[0], 0x90)\n        self.assertEqual(apdu[1], 0xE0)\n        self.assertEqual(apdu[5:7], ef['fid'])\n        self.assertEqual(apdu[7:9], list(ef['size'].to_bytes(2, 'big')))\n        self.assertEqual(apdu[9], ef['read_key'])\n        self.assertEqual(apdu[10], ef['write_key'])\n\n    def test_create_ef_file_fail_too_large(self):\n        ef = {'fid': [0x10, 0x03], 'size': 256, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x01}\n        response = create_ef_file(self.conn, ef['fid'], ef['size'], ef['read_key'], ef['write_key'])\n        self.assertEqual(response, ([], 0x6A, 0x84))\n\n    def test_write_ef_file_success(self):\n        ef = EF_FILES[0]\n        data = b'123456'\n        response = write_ef_file(self.conn, ef['fid'], 0, data)\n        # The last call should be WRITE BINARY\n        apdu = self.conn.transmit_calls[-1]\n        self.assertEqual(apdu[1], 0xD6)\n        self.assertEqual(apdu[4], len(data))\n        self.assertEqual(response, ([0x90, 0x00], 0x90, 0x00))\n\n    def test_write_ef_file_fail_zero_length(self):\n        ef = EF_FILES[0]\n        data = b''\n        response = write_ef_file(self.conn, ef['fid'], 0, data)\n        self.assertEqual(response, ([], 0x67, 0x00))\n\n    def test_read_ef_file_success(self):\n        ef = EF_FILES[0]\n        length = 8\n        response = read_ef_file(self.conn, ef['fid'], 0, length)\n        #                         "\"\"\"\nMIFARE Plus EV2 Personalization Script\n--------------------------------------\nThis script demonstrates how to personalize a MIFARE Plus EV2 card using an ACS ACR1552U reader.\nIt covers:\n    - Designing a simple EF (Elementary File) card file system structure\n    - Configuring access rights for files\n    - Performing read/write operations\n    - Integration with the ACS ACR1552U reader via PC/SC\n\nRequirements:\n    - pyscard (install with: pip install pyscard)\n    - ACS ACR1552U reader and MIFARE Plus EV2 card\n\nNote:\n    - This script uses ISO7816 APDU commands and MIFARE Plus EV2-specific commands.\n    - For real deployment, refer to NXP MIFARE Plus EV2 and ACS documentation.\n    - This example assumes the card is in SL3 (Security Level 3).\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom smartcard.System import readers\nfrom smartcard.util import toHexString, toBytes\n\n# ------------------- Configuration -------------------\n\n# Example EF file definition (File ID, Size, Access Rights)\nEF_FILES = [\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x01], 'size': 32, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x01},  # EF1\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x02], 'size': 64, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x02},  # EF2\n]\n\n# Example keys (16 bytes each, for demonstration only)\nKEYS = {\n    0x00: bytes.fromhex('000102030405060708090A0B0C0D0E0F'),\n    0x01: bytes.fromhex('101112131415161718191A1B1C1D1E1F'),\n    0x02: bytes.fromhex('202122232425262728292A2B2C2D2E2F'),\n}\n\n# ------------------- Utility Functions -------------------\n\ndef send_apdu(connection, apdu, expect_response=True):\n    \"\"\"\n    Send APDU command to the card and print response.\n    Returns:\n        - response (list of bytes)\n        - sw1, sw2 (status words)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"-> {toHexString(apdu)}\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = connection.transmit(apdu)\n    print(f\"<- {toHexString(response)} SW1={hex(sw1)} SW2={hex(sw2)}\")\n    if expect_response:\n        return response, sw1, sw2\n    else:\n        return sw1, sw2\n\ndef select_application(connection, aid):\n    \"\"\"\n    Select application by AID.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        aid: list of bytes representing the AID\n    \"\"\"\n    apdu = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x04, 0x00, len(aid)] + aid\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef authenticate_ev2(connection, key_no, key):\n    \"\"\"\n    EV2 First authentication (simplified).\n    In real use, this involves a challenge-response protocol.\n    Here, we use the ISO 7816 EXTERNAL AUTHENTICATE command as a placeholder.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        key_no: key number (int)\n        key: bytes object (16 bytes)\n    \"\"\"\n    # This is a placeholder for demonstration only.\n    apdu = [0x00, 0x82, 0x00, key_no, len(key)] + list(key)\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef create_ef_file(connection, fid, size, read_key, write_key):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create EF file using proprietary command.\n    For demonstration, we use a pseudo-APDU.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        fid: list of two bytes (file identifier)\n        size: int (file size in bytes)\n        read_key: int (key number for read access)\n        write_key: int (key number for write access)\n    \"\"\"\n    # Example: CLA INS P1 P2 Lc Data\n    # Data: FID(2) | Size(2) | ReadKey(1) | WriteKey(1)\n    size_bytes = size.to_bytes(2, 'big')\n    data = fid + list(size_bytes) + [read_key, write_key]\n    apdu = [0x90, 0xE0, 0x00, 0x00, len(data)] + data + [0x00]\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef write_ef_file(connection, fid, offset, data):\n    \"\"\"\n    Write data to EF file.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        fid: list of two bytes (file identifier)\n        offset: int (offset in file to write)\n        data: bytes object (data to write)\n    \"\"\"\n    # Select EF file\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    # Write Binary\n    apdu_write = [0x00, 0xD6, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, len(data)] + list(data)\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_write)\n\ndef read_ef_file(connection, fid, offset, length):\n    \"\"\"\n    Read data from EF file.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        fid: list of two bytes (file identifier)\n        offset: int (offset in file to read)\n        length: int (number of bytes to read)\n    Returns:\n        response (list of bytes), sw1, sw2\n    \"\"\"\n    # Select EF file\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    # Read Binary\n    apdu_read = [0x00, 0xB0, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, length]\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_read)\n\n# ------------------- Main Personalization Flow -------------------\n\ndef main():\n    # List readers\n    rlist = readers()\n    if not rlist:\n        print(\"No smart card readers found.\")\n        return\n    print(\"Available readers:\")\n    for idx, reader in enumerate(rlist):\n        print(f\"{idx}: {reader}\")\n\n    # Use first reader\n    reader = rlist[0]\n    print(f\"Using reader: {reader}\")\n\n    # Connect to card\n    connection = reader.createConnection()\n    try:\n        connection.connect()\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Failed to connect to card: {e}\")\n        return\n    print(\"Card connected.\")\n\n    # Select MIFARE application (AID is card-specific, example: 0xD2760000850101)\n    aid = [0xD2, 0x76, 0x00, 0x00, 0x85, 0x01, 0x01]\n    print(\"Selecting MIFARE application...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = select_application(connection, aid)\n    if sw1 != 0x90 and sw1 != 0x61:\n        print(\"Failed to select application. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Authenticate with master key (key 0x00)\n    print(\"Authenticating with master key...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(connection, 0x00, KEYS[0x00])\n    if sw1 != 0x90 and sw1 != 0x61:\n        print(\"Authentication failed. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Create EF files\n    for ef in EF_FILES:\n        print(f\"Creating EF file FID={toHexString(ef['fid'])}, Size={ef['size']}\")\n        response, sw1, sw2 = create_ef_file(connection, ef['fid'], ef['size'], ef['read_key'], ef['write_key'])\n        if sw1 != 0x90 and sw1 != 0x61:\n            print(\"Failed to create EF file {}. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(toHexString(ef['fid']), hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n            connection.disconnect()\n            return\n\n    # Write test data to EF1\n    test_data = b'Hello, MIFARE Plus EV2!'\n    print(f\"Writing to EF1: {test_data}\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(connection, EF_FILES[0]['write_key'], KEYS[EF_FILES[0]['write_key']])\n    if sw1 != 0x90 and sw1 != 0x61:\n        print(\"Write authentication failed. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    response, sw1, sw2 = write_ef_file(connection, EF_FILES[0]['fid'], 0, test_data)\n    if sw1 != 0x90 and sw1 != 0x61:\n        print(\"Failed to write to EF1. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Read back data from EF1\n    print(\"Reading from EF1...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(connection, EF_FILES[0]['read_key'], KEYS[EF_FILES[0]['read_key']])\n    if sw1 != 0x90 and sw1 != 0x61:\n        print(\"Read authentication failed. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    response, sw1, sw2 = read_ef_file(connection, EF_FILES[0]['fid'], 0, len(test_data))\n    if sw1 != 0x90 and sw1 != 0x61:\n        print(\"Failed to read from EF1. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    print(\"Read data:\", bytes(response).decode(errors='ignore'))\n\n    # Disconnect\n    connection.disconnect()\n    print(\"Personalization complete.\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n\n\"\"\"\nIntegration Notes for ACS ACR1552U:\n-----------------------------------\n- This script uses the PC/SC interface via pyscard, which is supported by the ACR1552U.\n- Ensure the ACR1552U driver is installed and the reader is recognized by your OS.\n- For advanced MIFARE Plus EV2 features (e.g., secure messaging, file management), refer to the NXP and ACS command sets.\n- For production, use secure key management and handle authentication/response as per NXP's documentation.\n\"\"\"",

                        "\"\"\"\nMIFARE Plus EV2 Personalization Script\n--------------------------------------\nThis script demonstrates how to personalize a MIFARE Plus EV2 card using an ACS ACR1552U reader.\nIt covers:\n    - Designing a simple EF (Elementary File) card file system structure\n    - Configuring access rights for files\n    - Performing read/write operations\n    - Integration with the ACS ACR1552U reader via PC/SC\n\nRequirements:\n    - pyscard (install with: pip install pyscard)\n    - ACS ACR1552U reader and MIFARE Plus EV2 card\n\nNote:\n    - This script uses ISO7816 APDU commands and MIFARE Plus EV2-specific commands.\n    - For real deployment, refer to NXP MIFARE Plus EV2 and ACS documentation.\n    - This example assumes the card is in SL3 (Security Level 3).\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom smartcard.System import readers\nfrom smartcard.util import toHexString, toBytes\nimport sys\n\n# ------------------- Configuration -------------------\n\n# Example EF file definition (File ID, Size, Access Rights)\nEF_FILES = [\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x01], 'size': 32, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x01},  # EF1\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x02], 'size': 64, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x02},  # EF2\n]\n\n# Example keys (16 bytes each, for demonstration only)\nKEYS = {\n    0x00: bytes.fromhex('000102030405060708090A0B0C0D0E0F'),\n    0x01: bytes.fromhex('101112131415161718191A1B1C1D1E1F'),\n    0x02: bytes.fromhex('202122232425262728292A2B2C2D2E2F'),\n}\n\n# ------------------- Utility Functions -------------------\n\ndef send_apdu(connection, apdu, expect_response=True):\n    \"\"\"\n    Send APDU to the card and print the response.\n    Returns response data and status words.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"-> {toHexString(apdu)}\")\n    try:\n        response, sw1, sw2 = connection.transmit(apdu)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"APDU transmission error: {e}\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n    print(f\"<- {toHexString(response)} SW1={hex(sw1)} SW2={hex(sw2)}\")\n    if expect_response:\n        return response, sw1, sw2\n    else:\n        return sw1, sw2\n\ndef select_application(connection, aid):\n    \"\"\"\n    Select application by AID.\n    Returns response, sw1, sw2.\n    \"\"\"\n    apdu = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x04, 0x00, len(aid)] + aid\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef authenticate_ev2(connection, key_no, key):\n    \"\"\"\n    EV2 First authentication (simplified).\n    In real use, this involves a challenge-response protocol.\n    Here, we use the ISO 7816 EXTERNAL AUTHENTICATE command as a placeholder.\n    Returns response, sw1, sw2.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Select EF file\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    # Write Binary\n    apdu_write = [0x00, 0xD6, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, len(data)] + list(data)\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_write)\n\ndef read_ef_file(connection, fid, offset, length):\n    \"\"\"\n    Read data from EF file.\n    Selects the EF file, then reads data at the specified offset.\n    Returns response, sw1, sw2.\n    \"\"\"\n    # List PC/SC readers\n    rlist = readers()\n    if not rlist:\n        print(\"No smart card readers found.\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n    print(\"Available readers:\")\n    for idx, reader in enumerate(rlist):\n        print(f\"{idx}: {reader}\")\n\n    # Use first reader\n    reader = rlist[0]\n    print(f\"Using reader: {reader}\")\n\n    # Connect to card\n    try:\n        connection = reader.createConnection()\n        connection.connect()\n        print(\"Card connected.\")\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Failed to connect to card: {e}\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # Select MIFARE application (AID is card-specific, example: 0xD2760000850101)\n    aid = [0xD2, 0x76, 0x00, 0x00, 0x85, 0x01, 0x01]\n    print(\"Selecting MIFARE application...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = select_application(connection, aid)\n    if sw1 != 0x90 and sw1 != 0x61:\n        print(\"Failed to select application. SW1/SW2:\", hex(sw1), hex(sw2))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # Create EF files\n    for ef in EF_FILES:\n        print(f\"Creating EF file FID={toHexString(ef['fid'])}, Size={ef['size']}\")\n        response, sw1, sw2 = create_ef_file(connection, ef['fid'], ef['size'], ef['read_key'], ef['write_key'])\n        if sw1 != 0x90 and sw1 != 0x61:\n            print(f\"Failed to create EF file {toHexString(ef['fid'])}. select\n            ([ord('H'), ord('i')], 0x90, 0x00),  # read\n        ]\n        fid = [0x10, 0x01]\n        offset = 0\n        length = 2\n        response, sw1, sw2 = read_ef_file(self.connection, fid, offset, length)\n        self.assertEqual(response, [ord('H'), ord('i')])\n        self.assertEqual(sw1, 0x90)\n        self.assertEqual(sw2, 0x00)\n        expected_read = [0x00, 0xB0, 0x00, 0x00, length]\n        self.connection.transmit.assert_any_call(expected_read)\n\n    def test_read_ef_file_offset_edge(self):\n        for offset in [0, 0xFFFF]:\n            self.connection.transmit.side_effect = [\n                ([0x00], 0x90, 0x00),  # select\n                ([0x01], 0x90, 0x00),  # read\n            ]\n            fid = [0x10, 0x01]\n            length = 1\n            response, sw1, sw2 = read_ef_file(self.connection, fid, offset, length)\n            self.assertEqual(response, [0x01])\n            self.assertEqual(sw1, 0x90)\n            self.assertEqual(sw2, 0x00)\n            expected_read = [0x00, 0xB0, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, length]\n            self.connection.transmit.assert_any_call(expected_read)\n\n    def test_read_ef_file_too_large(self):\n        self.connection.transmit.side_effect = [\n            ([0x00], 0x90, 0x00),  # select\n            ([0x00], 0x6C, 0x00),  # read: error\n        ]\n        fid = [0x10, 0x01]\n        offset = 0\n        length = EF_FILES[0]['size'] + 10  # 32+10=42, file size is 32\n        response, sw1, sw2 = read_ef_file(self.connection, fid, offset, length)\n        self.assertEqual(response, [0x00])\n        self.assertEqual(sw1, 0x6C)  # SW1=0x6C indicates wrong length\n        self.assertEqual(sw2, 0x00)\n\n    def test_send_apdu_expect_response_false(self):\n        self.connection.transmit.return_value = ([0x01, 0x02], 0x90, 0x00)\n        apdu = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x04, 0x00, 0x07, 0xD2, 0x76, 0x00, 0x00, 0x85, 0x01, 0x01]\n        sw1, sw2 = send_apdu(self.connection, apdu, expect_response=False)\n        self.assertEqual(sw1, 0x90)\n        self.assertEqual(sw2, 0x00)\n\n    def test_apdu_format(self):\n        # Ensure APDU is correctly formatted for select_application\n        aid = [0xD2, 0x76, 0x00, 0x00, 0x85, 0x01, 0x01]\n        with patch('builtins.print'):\n            select_application(self.connection, aid)\n        expected_apdu = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x04, 0x00, len(aid)] + aid\n        self.connection.transmit.assert_called_with(expected_apdu)\n\n    def test_authenticate_ev2_apdu_length(self):\n        # Test with a key of incorrect length (should still send, but APDU will be wrong)\n        self.connection.transmit.return_value = ([0x00], 0x90, 0x00)\n        key_no = 0x01\n        key = b'\\x01\\x02\\x03'  # wrong length\n        response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(self.connection, key_no, key)\n        expected_apdu = [0x00, 0x82, 0x00, key_no, len(key)] + list(key)\n        self.connection.transmit.assert_called_with(expected_apdu)\n        self.assertEqual(response, [0x00])\n        self.assertEqual(sw1, 0x90)\n        self.assertEqual(sw2, 0x00)\n\n    def test_create_ef_file_invalid_fid(self):\n        # select\n            ([], 0x90, 0x00),  # read\n        ]\n        fid = [0x10, 0x01]\n        offset = 0\n        length = 0\n        response, sw1, sw2 = read_ef_file(self.connection, fid, offset, length)\n        expected_read = [0x00, 0xB0, 0x00, 0x00, 0]\n        self.connection.transmit.assert_any_call(expected_read)\n        self.assertEqual(response, [])\n        self.assertEqual(sw1, 0x90)\n        self.assertEqual(sw2, 0x00)\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    unittest.main()",
                        "import unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import MagicMock, patch\n\n# Import functions from the provided script\n# We'll assume the script is named mifare_ev2.py and functions are bytes.fromhex('101112131415161718191A1B1C1D1E1F'),\n    0x02: bytes.fromhex('202122232425262728292A2B2C2D2E2F'),\n}\n\ndef send_apdu(connection, apdu, expect_response=True):\n    \"\"\"\n    Send APDU authenticate_ev2(connection, key_no, key):\n    \"\"\"\n    EV2 First authentication (simplified).\n    In real use, this involves a challenge-response protocol.\n    Here, we use the ISO 7816   \"\"\"\n    Write data to EF file.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        fid: list of two bytes (file identifier)\n        offset: int (offset in file to write)\n        data: bytes object (data to write)\n    \"\"\"\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    apdu_write = [0x00, 0xD6, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, len(data)] + list(data)\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_write)\n\ndef read_ef_file(connection, fid, offset, length):\n    \"\"\"\n    Read data from EF file.\n    Args:\n    response (list of bytes), sw1, sw2\n    \"\"\"\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    apdu_read = [0x00, 0xB0, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, length]\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_read)\n\n# ------------------- End Functions Under Test -------------------\n\nclass DummyConnection:\n    \"\"\"\n    A dummy connection object to simulate pyscard's transmit behavior.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.last_apdu = None\n        self.ef_storage = {\n            tuple(EF_FILES[0]['fid']): bytearray(EF_FILES[0]['size']),\n            tuple(EF_FILES[1]['fid']): bytearray(EF_FILES[1]['size']),\n        }\n        self.selected_fid = None\n\n    def transmit(self, apdu):\n        self.last_apdu = apdu\n        # Simulate APDU responses based on command\n        cla, ins = apdu[0], apdu[1]\n        # Select Application\n        if cla == 0x00 and ins == 0xA4 and apdu[2] == 0x04:\n            # Application selection success\n            return ([], 0x90, 0x00)\n        # Authenticate\n        elif cla == 0x00 and ins == 0x82:\n            # Accept any key, always succeed for test\n            return ([], 0x90, 0x00)\n        # Create EF file\n        elif cla == 0x90 and ins == 0xE0:\n            fid = tuple(apdu[5:7])\n            size = int.from_bytes(apdu[7:9], 'big')\n            self.ef_storage[fid] = bytearray(size)\n            return ([], 0x90, 0x00)\n        # Select EF file\n        elif cla == 0x00 and ins == 0xA4 and apdu[2] == 0x00:\n            fid = tuple(apdu[5:7])\n            if fid in self.ef_storage:\n                self.selected_fid = fid\n                return ([], 0x90, 0x00)\n            else:\n                return ([], 0x6A, 0x82)  # File not found\n        # Write Binary\n        elif cla == 0x00 and ins == 0xD6:\n            if self.selected_fid is None:\n                return ([], 0x69, 0x86)  # Command not allowed\n            offset = (apdu[2] << 8) | apdu[3]\n            length = apdu[4]\n            data = apdu[5:5+length]\n            ef = self.ef_storage[self.selected_fid]\n            if offset + length > len(ef):\n                return ([], 0x67, 0x00)  # Wrong length\n            ef[offset:offset+length] = data\n            return ([], 0x90, 0x00)\n        # Read Binary\n        elif cla == 0x00 and ins == 0xB0:\n            if self.selected_fid is None:\n                return ([], 0x69, 0x86)\n            offset = (apdu[2] << 8) | apdu[3]\n            length = apdu[4]\n            ef = self.ef_storage[self.selected_fid]\n            if offset + length > len(ef):\n                return ([], 0x67, 0x00)\n            return (list(ef[offset:offset+length]), 0x90, 0x00)\n        # Default: unknown command\n        return ([], 0x6D, 0x00)\n\nclass TestMifarePlusEV2Personalization(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.connection = DummyConnection()\n\n    def                         "\"\"\"\nMIFARE Plus EV2 Personalization Script\n--------------------------------------\nThis script demonstrates how to personalize a MIFARE Plus EV2 card using an ACS ACR1552U reader.\nFeatures:\n    - EF (Elementary File) card file system design\n    - Access rights configuration for files\n    - Read/write operations\n    - Integration with ACS ACR1552U via PC/SC (pyscard)\n\nRequirements:\n    - pyscard (pip install pyscard)\n    - ACS ACR1552U reader and MIFARE Plus EV2 card\n\nNote:\n    - Uses ISO7816 APDU and MIFARE Plus EV2-like commands.\n    - For real deployment, consult NXP MIFARE Plus EV2 and ACS documentation.\n    - Assumes card is in SL3 (Security Level 3).\n    - This is a demonstration; adapt for production use.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom smartcard.System import readers\nfrom smartcard.util import toHexString, toBytes\n\n# ------------------- Configuration -------------------\n\n# EF file system: list of dicts with File ID, Size, Access Rights\nEF_FILES = [\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x01], 'size': 32, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x01},  # EF1\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x02], 'size': 64, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x02},  # EF2\n]\n\n# Example keys (16 bytes each, for demonstration only)\nKEYS = {\n    0x00: bytes.fromhex('000102030405060708090A0B0C0D0E0F'),\n    0x01: bytes.fromhex('101112131415161718191A1B1C1D1E1F'),\n    0x02: bytes.fromhex('202122232425262728292A2B2C2D2E2F'),\n}\n\n# ------------------- Utility Functions -------------------\n\ndef send_apdu(connection, apdu, expect_response=True):\n    \"\"\"\n    Send APDU command to the card and print response.\n    Returns:\n        - response (list of bytes)\n        - sw1, sw2 (status words)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"-> {toHexString(apdu)}\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = connection.transmit(apdu)\n    print(f\"<- {toHexString(response)} SW1={hex(sw1)} SW2={hex(sw2)}\")\n    if expect_response:\n        return response, sw1, sw2\n    else:\n        return sw1, sw2\n\ndef select_application(connection, aid):\n    \"\"\"\n    Select application by AID.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        aid: list of bytes representing the AID\n    \"\"\"\n    apdu = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x04, 0x00, len(aid)] + aid\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef authenticate_ev2(connection, key_no, key):\n    \"\"\"\n    EV2 First authentication (simplified).\n    In real use, this involves a challenge-response protocol.\n    Here, we use the ISO 7816 EXTERNAL AUTHENTICATE command as a placeholder.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        key_no: key number (int)\n        key: bytes object (16 bytes)\n    \"\"\"\n    # This is a placeholder for demonstration only.\n    apdu = [0x00, 0x82, 0x00, key_no, len(key)] + list(key)\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef create_ef_file(connection, fid, size, read_key, write_key):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create EF file using proprietary command.\n    For demonstration, we use a pseudo-APDU.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        fid: list of two bytes (file identifier)\n        size: int (file size in bytes)\n        read_key: int (key number for read access)\n        write_key: int (key number for write access)\n    \"\"\"\n    # Example: CLA INS P1 P2 Lc Data\n    # Data: FID(2) | Size(2) | ReadKey(1) | WriteKey(1)\n    size_bytes = size.to_bytes(2, 'big')\n    data = fid + list(size_bytes) + [read_key, write_key]\n    apdu = [0x90, 0xE0, 0x00, 0x00, len(data)] + data + [0x00]\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef write_ef_file(connection, fid, offset, data):\n    \"\"\"\n    Write data to EF file.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        fid: list of two bytes (file identifier)\n        offset: int (offset in file to write)\n        data: bytes object (data to write)\n    \"\"\"\n    # Select EF file\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    # Write Binary\n    apdu_write = [0x00, 0xD6, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, len(data)] + list(data)\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_write)\n\ndef read_ef_file(connection, fid, offset, length):\n    \"\"\"\n    Read data from EF file.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        fid: list of two bytes (file identifier)\n        offset: int (offset in file to read)\n        length: int (number of bytes to read)\n    Returns:\n        response (list of bytes), sw1, sw2\n    \"\"\"\n    # Select EF file\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    # Read Binary\n    apdu_read = [0x00, 0xB0, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, length]\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_read)\n\n# ------------------- Main Personalization Flow -------------------\n\ndef main():\n    # List readers\n    rlist = readers()\n    if not rlist:\n        print(\"No smart card readers found.\")\n        return\n    print(\"Available readers:\")\n    for idx, reader in enumerate(rlist):\n        print(f\"{idx}: {reader}\")\n\n    # Use first reader\n    reader = rlist[0]\n    print(f\"Using reader: {reader}\")\n\n    # Connect to card\n    connection = reader.createConnection()\n    try:\n        connection.connect()\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Failed to connect to card: {e}\")\n        return\n    print(\"Card connected.\")\n\n    # Select MIFARE application (AID is card-specific, example: 0xD2760000850101)\n    aid = [0xD2, 0x76, 0x00, 0x00, 0x85, 0x01, 0x01]\n    print(\"Selecting MIFARE application...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = select_application(connection, aid)\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Failed to select application. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Authenticate with master key (key 0x00)\n    print(\"Authenticating with master key...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(connection, 0x00, KEYS[0x00])\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Authentication failed. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Create EF files\n    for ef in EF_FILES:\n        print(f\"Creating EF file FID={toHexString(ef['fid'])}, Size={ef['size']}\")\n        response, sw1, sw2 = create_ef_file(connection, ef['fid'], ef['size'], ef['read_key'], ef['write_key'])\n        if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n            print(\"Failed to create EF file {}. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(toHexString(ef['fid']), hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n            connection.disconnect()\n            return\n\n    # Write test data to EF1\n    test_data = b'Hello, MIFARE Plus EV2!'\n    print(f\"Writing to EF1: {test_data}\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(connection, EF_FILES[0]['write_key'], KEYS[EF_FILES[0]['write_key']])\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Write authentication failed. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    response, sw1, sw2 = write_ef_file(connection, EF_FILES[0]['fid'], 0, test_data)\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Failed to write to EF1. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Read back data from EF1\n    print(\"Reading from EF1...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(connection, EF_FILES[0]['read_key'], KEYS[EF_FILES[0]['read_key']])\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Read authentication failed. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    response, sw1, sw2 = read_ef_file(connection, EF_FILES[0]['fid'], 0, len(test_data))\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Failed to read from EF1. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    print(\"Read data:\", bytes(response).decode(errors='ignore'))\n\n    # Disconnect\n    connection.disconnect()\n    print(\"Personalization complete.\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n\n\"\"\"\nIntegration Notes for ACS ACR1552U:\n-----------------------------------\n- This script uses the PC/SC interface via pyscard, which is supported by the ACR1552U.\n- Ensure the ACR1552U driver is installed and the reader is recognized by your OS.\n- For advanced MIFARE Plus EV2 features (secure messaging, file management), refer to NXP and ACS command sets.\n- For production, use secure key management and handle authentication/response as per NXP's documentation.\n\"\"\"",
                        "\"\"\"\nMIFARE Plus EV2 Personalization Script\n--------------------------------------\nThis script demonstrates how to personalize a MIFARE Plus EV2 card using an ACS ACR1552U reader.\nIt covers:\n    - Designing a simple EF (Elementary File) card file system structure\n    - Configuring access rights for files\n    - Performing read/write operations\n    - Integration with the ACS ACR1552U reader via PC/SC\n\nRequirements:\n    - pyscard (install with: pip install pyscard)\n    - ACS ACR1552U reader and MIFARE Plus EV2 card\n\nNote:\n    - This script uses ISO7816 APDU commands and MIFARE Plus EV2-specific commands.\n    - For real deployment, refer to NXP MIFARE Plus EV2 and ACS documentation.\n    - This example assumes the card is in SL3 (Security Level 3).\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom smartcard.System import readers\nfrom smartcard.util import toHexString, toBytes\n\n# ------------------- Configuration -------------------\n\n# Example EF file definition (File ID, Size, Access Rights)\nEF_FILES = [\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x01], 'size': 32, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x01},  # EF1\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x02], 'size': 64, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x02},  # EF2\n]\n\n# Example keys (16 bytes each, for demonstration only)\nKEYS = {\n    0x00: bytes.fromhex('000102030405060708090A0B0C0D0E0F'),\n    0x01: bytes.fromhex('101112131415161718191A1B1C1D1E1F'),\n    0x02: bytes.fromhex('202122232425262728292A2B2C2D2E2F'),\n}\n\n# ------------------- Utility Functions -------------------\n\ndef send_apdu(connection, apdu, expect_response=True):\n    \"\"\"\n    Send APDU command to the card and print response.\n    Returns:\n        - response (list of bytes)\n        - sw1, sw2 (status words)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"-> {toHexString(apdu)}\")\n    try:\n        response, sw1, sw2 = connection.transmit(apdu)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"APDU transmission error: {e}\")\n        return [], 0x00, 0x00\n    print(f\"<- {toHexString(response)} SW1={hex(sw1)} SW2={hex(sw2)}\")\n    if expect_response:\n        return response, sw1, sw2\n    else:\n        return sw1, sw2\n\ndef select_application(connection, aid):\n    \"\"\"\n    Select application by AID.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        aid: list of bytes representing the AID\n    \"\"\"\n    apdu = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x04, 0x00, len(aid)] + aid\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef authenticate_ev2(connection, key_no, key):\n    \"\"\"\n    EV2 First authentication (simplified).\n    In real use, this involves a challenge-response protocol.\n    Here, we use the ISO 7816 EXTERNAL AUTHENTICATE command as a placeholder.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        key_no: key number (int)\n        key: bytes object (16 bytes)\n    \"\"\"\n    # This is a placeholder for demonstration only.\n    apdu = [0x00, 0x82, 0x00, key_no, len(key)] + list(key)\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef create_ef_file(connection, fid, size, read_key, write_key):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create EF file using proprietary command.\n    For demonstration, we use a pseudo-APDU.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        fid: list of two bytes (file identifier)\n        size: int (file size in bytes)\n        read_key: int (key number for read access)\n        write_key: int (key number for write access)\n    \"\"\"\n    # Example: CLA INS P1 P2 Lc Data\n    # Data: FID(2) | Size(2) | ReadKey(1) | WriteKey(1)\n    size_bytes = size.to_bytes(2, 'big')\n    data = fid + list(size_bytes) + [read_key, write_key]\n    apdu = [0x90, 0xE0, 0x00, 0x00, len(data)] + data + [0x00]\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef write_ef_file(connection, fid, offset, data):\n    \"\"\"\n    Write data to EF file.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        fid: list of two bytes (file identifier)\n        offset: int (offset in file to write)\n        data: bytes object (data to write)\n    \"\"\"\n    # Select EF file\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    # Write Binary\n    apdu_write = [0x00, 0xD6, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, len(data)] + list(data)\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_write)\n\ndef read_ef_file(connection, fid, offset, length):\n    \"\"\"\n    Read data from EF file.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        fid: list of two bytes (file identifier)\n        offset: int (offset in file to read)\n        length: int (number of bytes to read)\n    Returns:\n        response (list of bytes), sw1, sw2\n    \"\"\"\n    # Select EF file\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    # Read Binary\n    apdu_read = [0x00, 0xB0, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, length]\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_read)\n\n# ------------------- Main Personalization Flow -------------------\n\ndef main():\n    # List readers\n    rlist = readers()\n    if not rlist:\n        print(\"No smart card readers found.\")\n        return\n    print(\"Available readers:\")\n    for idx, reader in enumerate(rlist):\n        print(f\"{idx}: {reader}\")\n\n    # Use first reader\n    reader = rlist[0]\n    print(f\"Using reader: {reader}\")\n\n    # Connect to card\n    connection = reader.createConnection()\n    try:\n        connection.connect()\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Failed to connect to card: {e}\")\n        return\n    print(\"Card connected.\")\n\n    # Select MIFARE application (AID is card-specific, example: 0xD2760000850101)\n    aid = [0xD2, 0x76, 0x00, 0x00, 0x85, 0x01, 0x01]\n    print(\"Selecting MIFARE application...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = select_application(connection, aid)\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Failed to select application. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Authenticate with master key (key 0x00)\n    print(\"Authenticating with master key...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(connection, 0x00, KEYS[0x00])\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Authentication failed. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Create EF files\n    for ef in EF_FILES:\n        print(f\"Creating EF file FID={toHexString(ef['fid'])}, Size={ef['size']}\")\n        response, sw1, sw2 = create_ef_file(connection, ef['fid'], ef['size'], ef['read_key'], ef['write_key'])\n        if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n            print(\"Failed to create EF file {}. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(toHexString(ef['fid']), hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n            connection.disconnect()\n            return\n\n    # Write test data to EF1\n    test_data = b'Hello, MIFARE Plus EV2!'\n    print(f\"Writing to EF1: {test_data}\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(connection, EF_FILES[0]['write_key'], KEYS[EF_FILES[0]['write_key']])\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Write authentication failed. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    response, sw1, sw2 = write_ef_file(connection, EF_FILES[0]['fid'], 0, test_data)\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Failed to write to EF1. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Read back data from EF1\n    print(\"Reading from EF1...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(connection, EF_FILES[0]['read_key'], KEYS[EF_FILES[0]['read_key']])\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Read authentication failed. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    response, sw1, sw2 = read_ef_file(connection, EF_FILES[0]['fid'], 0, len(test_data))\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Failed to read from EF1. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    print(\"Read data:\", bytes(response).decode(errors='ignore'))\n\n    # Disconnect\n    connection.disconnect()\n    print(\"Personalization complete.\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n\n\"\"\"\nIntegration Notes for ACS ACR1552U:\n-----------------------------------\n- This script uses the PC/SC interface via pyscard, which is supported by the ACR1552U.\n- Ensure the ACR1552U driver is installed and the reader is recognized by your OS.\n- For advanced MIFARE Plus EV2 features (e.g., secure messaging, file management), refer to the NXP and ACS command sets.\n- For production, use secure key management and handle authentication/response as per NXP's documentation.\n\"\"\"",
                        "\"\"\"\nMIFARE Plus EV2 Personalization Script\n--------------------------------------\nThis script demonstrates how to personalize a MIFARE Plus EV2 card using an ACS ACR1552U reader.\nIt covers:\n    - Designing a simple EF (Elementary File) card file system structure\n    - Configuring access rights for files\n    - Performing read/write operations\n    - Integration with the ACS ACR1552U reader via PC/SC\n\nRequirements:\n    - pyscard (install with: pip install pyscard)\n    - ACS ACR1552U reader and MIFARE Plus EV2 card\n\nNote:\n    - This script uses ISO7816 APDU commands and MIFARE Plus EV2-specific commands.\n    - For real deployment, refer to NXP MIFARE Plus EV2 and ACS documentation.\n    - This example assumes the card is in SL3 (Security Level 3).\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom smartcard.System import readers\nfrom smartcard.util import toHexString, toBytes\n\n# ------------------- Configuration -------------------\n\n# Example EF file definition (File ID, Size, Access Rights)\nEF_FILES = [\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x01], 'size': 32, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x01},  # EF1\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x02], 'size': 64, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x02},  # EF2\n]\n\n# Example keys (16 bytes each, for demonstration only)\nKEYS = {\n    0x00: bytes.fromhex('000102030405060708090A0B0C0D0E0F'),\n    0x01: bytes.fromhex('101112131415161718191A1B1C1D1E1F'),\n    0x02: bytes.fromhex('202122232425262728292A2B2C2D2E2F'),\n}\n\n# ------------------- Utility Functions -------------------\n\ndef send_apdu(connection, apdu, expect_response=True):\n    \"\"\"\n    Send APDU command to the card and print response.\n    Returns:\n        - response (list of bytes)\n        - sw1, sw2 (status words)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"-> {toHexString(apdu)}\")\n    try:\n        response, sw1, sw2 = connection.transmit(apdu)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"APDU transmit error: {e}\")\n        return [], 0x6F, 0x00  # SW1=0x6F: Command aborted\n    print(f\"<- {toHexString(response)} SW1={hex(sw1)} SW2={hex(sw2)}\")\n    if expect_response:\n        return response, sw1, sw2\n    else:\n        return sw1, sw2\n\ndef select_application(connection, aid):\n    \"\"\"\n    Select application by AID.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        aid: list of bytes representing the AID\n    \"\"\"\n    apdu = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x04, 0x00, len(aid)] + aid\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef authenticate_ev2(connection, key_no, key):\n    \"\"\"\n    EV2 First authentication (simplified).\n    In real use, this involves a challenge-response protocol.\n    Here, we use the ISO 7816 EXTERNAL AUTHENTICATE command as a placeholder.\n    Args:\n        connection: pyscard connection object\n        key_no: key number (int)\n        key: bytes object (16 bytes)\n    \"\"\"\n    # Select EF file\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    # Read Binary\n    apdu_read = [0x00, 0xB0, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, length]\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_read)\n\n# ------------------- Main Personalization Flow -------------------\n\ndef main():\n    # Select MIFARE application (AID is card-specific, example: 0xD2760000850101)\n    aid = [0xD2, 0x76, 0x00, 0x00, 0x85, 0x01, 0x01]\n    print(\"Selecting MIFARE application...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = select_application(connection, aid)\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Failed to select application. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Create EF files\n    for ef in EF_FILES:\n        print(f\"Creating EF file FID={toHexString(ef['fid'])}, Size={ef['size']}\")\n        response, sw1, sw2 = create_ef_file(connection, ef['fid'], ef['size'], ef['read_key'], ef['write_key'])\n        if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n            print(\"Failed to create EF file {}.                         "import unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import MagicMock, patch\n\n# Import the code to test\n# For this test, we assume all functions are in the same script and accessible.\n# If the code is in a module, you would import them accordingly.\n\n# Copy the relevant functions and data from the provided code for testing\n# (simulate as if imported, but here we just define them for the test)\n\n# ------------------- Mocks and Data -------------------\n\nEF_FILES = [\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x01], 'size': 32, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x01},  # TestMifarePlusEV2Personalization(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a mock connection object\n        self.connection = MagicMock()\n        # Set up a simple card memory for EF files\n        # {fid: bytearray(size)}\n        self.card_memory = {\n            tuple(EF_FILES[0]['fid']): bytearray(EF_FILES[0]['size']),\n            tuple(EF_FILES[1]['fid']): bytearray(EF_FILES[1]['size']),\n        }\n        # Track selected file\n        self.selected_fid = None\n\n        # Patch transmit to simulate card behavior\n        def transmit_side_effect(apdu):\n            # Application selection\n            if apdu[:2] == [0x00, 0xA4]:\n                # Select application or file\n                if apdu[2] == 0x04:  # application select\n                    # Accept any AID\n                    return ([], 0x90, 0x00)\n                elif apdu[2] == 0x00:  # file select\n                    fid = tuple(apdu[-2:])\n                    if fid in self.card_memory:\n                        self.selected_fid = fid\n                        return ([], 0x90, 0x00)\n                    else:\n                        return ([], 0x6A, 0x82)  # file not found\n            # Authenticate\n            elif apdu[:2] == [0x00, 0x82]:\n                key_no = apdu[3]\n                key = bytes(apdu[5:21])\n                if key_no in KEYS and key == KEYS[key_no]:\n                    return ([], 0x90, 0x00)\n                else:\n                    return ([], 0x69, 0x82)  # authentication failed\n            # Create EF file\n            elif apdu[:2] == [0x90, 0xE0]:\n                fid = tuple(apdu[5:7])\n                size = int.from_bytes(apdu[7:9], 'big')\n                if fid not in self.card_memory:\n                    self.card_memory[fid] = bytearray(size)\n                    return ([], 0x90, 0x00)\n                else:\n                    return ([], 0x6A, 0x80)  # file already exists\n            # Write Binary\n            elif apdu[:2] == [0x00, 0xD6]:\n                if self.selected_fid is None:\n                    return ([], 0x69, 0x86)  # no file selected\n                offset = (apdu[2] << 8) | apdu[3]\n                length = apdu[4]\n                data = bytes(apdu[5:5+length])\n                mem = self.card_memory[self.selected_fid]\n                if offset + length > len(mem):\n                    return ([], 0x6B, 0x00)  # wrong parameters\n                mem[offset:offset+length] = data\n                return ([], 0x90, 0x00)\n            # Read Binary\n            elif apdu[:2] == [0x00, 0xB0]:\n                if self.selected_fid is None:\n                    return ([], 0x69, 0x86)\n                offset = (apdu[2] << 8) | apdu[3]\n                length = apdu[4]\n                mem = self.card_memory[self.selected_fid]\n                if offset + length > len(mem):\n                    return ([], 0x6B, 0x00)\n                data = list(mem[offset:offset+length])\n                return (data, 0x90, 0x00)\n            else:\n                return ([], 0x6D, 0x00)  # instruction not supported\n\n        self.connection.transmit.side_effect = transmit_side_effect\n\n    def test_select_application_success(self):\n        aid = [0xD2, 0x76, 0x00, 0x00, 0x85, 0x01, 0x01]\n        response, sw1, sw2 = select_application(self.connection, aid)\n        self.assertEqual((sw1, sw2), (0x90, 0x00))\n        self.assertEqual(response, [])\n\n    def test_select_file_success_and_failure(self):\n        # Select existing file\n        fid = EF_FILES[0]['fid']\n        apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n        response, sw1, sw2 = send_apdu(self.connection, apdu_select)\n        self.assertEqual((sw1, sw2), (0x90, 0x00))\n        # Select non-existing file\n        fid_bad = [0x99, 0x99]\n        apdu_select_bad = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid_bad\n        response, sw1, sw2 = send_apdu(self.connection, apdu_select_bad)\n        self.assertEqual((sw1, sw2), (0x6A, 0x82))\n\n    def test_authenticate_success_and_failure(self):\n        # Correct key\n        response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(self.connection, 0x00, KEYS[0x00])\n        self.assertEqual((sw1, sw2), (0x90, 0x00))\n        # Wrong key\n        wrong_key = b'\\xFF'*16\n        response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(self.connection, 0x00, wrong_key)\n        self.assertEqual((sw1, sw2), (0x69, 0x82))\n\n    def test_create_ef_file_success_and_duplicate(self):\n        # Create new file\n        fid_new = [0x20, 0x01]\n        size = 16\n        response, sw1, sw2 = create_ef_file(self.connection, fid_new, size, 0x00, 0x01)\n        self.assertEqual((sw1, sw2), (0x90, 0x00))\n        # Try to create again (duplicate)\n        response, sw1, sw2 = create_ef_file(self.connection, fid_new, size, 0x00, 0x01)\n        self.assertEqual((sw1, sw2), (0x6A, 0x80))\n\n    def test_write_and_read_ef_file(self):\n        fid = EF_FILES[0]['fid']\n        # Select file\n        apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n        send_apdu(self.connection, apdu_select)\n        # Write data\n        data = b'TestData123'\n        response, sw1, sw2 = write_ef_file(self.connection, fid, 0, data)\n        self.assertEqual((sw1, sw2), (0x90, 0x00))\n        # Read back\n        response, sw1, sw2 = read_ef_file(self.connection, fid, 0, len(data))\n        self.assertEqual((sw1, sw2), (0x90, 0x00))\n        self.assertEqual(bytes(response), data)\n\n    def test_write_out_of_bounds(self):\n        fid = EF_FILES[0]['fid']\n        apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n        send_apdu(self.connection, apdu_select)\n        # Write data beyond file size\n        data = b'A' * (EF_FILES[0]['size'] + 1)\n        response, sw1, sw2 = SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Create EF files\n    for ef in EF_FILES:\n        print(f\"Creating EF file FID={toHexString(ef['fid'])}, Size={ef['size']}\")\n        response, sw1, sw2 = create_ef_file(connection, ef['fid'], ef['size'], ef['read_key'], ef['write_key'])\n        if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n            print(\"Failed to create EF file {}. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(toHexString(ef['fid']), hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n            connection.disconnect()\n            return\n\n    # Write test data to EF1\n    test_data = b'Hello, MIFARE Plus EV2!'\n    print(f\"Writing to EF1: {test_data}\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(connection, EF_FILES[0]['write_key'], KEYS[EF_FILES[0]['write_key']])\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Write authentication failed. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    response, sw1, sw2 = write_ef_file(connection, EF_FILES[0]['fid'], 0, test_data)\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Failed to write to EF1. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n\n    # Read back data from EF1\n    print(\"Reading from EF1...\")\n    response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(connection, EF_FILES[0]['read_key'], KEYS[EF_FILES[0]['read_key']])\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Read authentication failed. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    response, sw1, sw2 = read_ef_file(connection, EF_FILES[0]['fid'], 0, len(test_data))\n    if sw1 not in (0x90, 0x61):\n        print(\"Failed to read from EF1. SW1={}, SW2={}\".format(hex(sw1), hex(sw2)))\n        connection.disconnect()\n        return\n    print(\"Read data:\", bytes(response).decode(errors='ignore'))\n\n    # Disconnect\n    connection.disconnect()\n    print(\"Personalization complete.\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n\n\"\"\"\nIntegration Notes for ACS ACR1552U:\n-----------------------------------\n- This script uses the PC/SC interface via pyscard, which is supported by the ACR1552U.\n- Ensure the ACR1552U driver is installed and the reader is recognized by your OS.\n- For advanced MIFARE Plus EV2 features (secure messaging, file management), refer to NXP and ACS command sets.\n- For production, use secure key management and handle authentication/response as per NXP's documentation.\n\"\"\"",
                    "best_tests": "import unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import MagicMock, patch\n\n# Import functions and constants from the original script\n# For this test suite, we assume the script is named 'mifare_ev2.py'\n# and all relevant functions/constants are imported as below.\n# If the code is in the same file, comment out the import lines.\n\n# from mifare_ev2 import (\n#     send_apdu, select_application, authenticate_ev2,\n#     create_ef_file, write_ef_file, read_ef_file,\n#     EF_FILES, KEYS\n# )\n\n# For demonstration, copy the relevant functions and constants here.\n# Remove all print statements for cleaner test output.\n\nEF_FILES = [\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x01], 'size': 32, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x01},  # EF1\n    {'fid': [0x10, 0x02], 'size': 64, 'read_key': 0x00, 'write_key': 0x02},  # EF2\n]\n\nKEYS = {\n    0x00: bytes.fromhex('000102030405060708090A0B0C0D0E0F'),\n    0x01: bytes.fromhex('101112131415161718191A1B1C1D1E1F'),\n    0x02: bytes.fromhex('202122232425262728292A2B2C2D2E2F'),\n}\n\ndef send_apdu(connection, apdu, expect_response=True):\n    response, sw1, sw2 = connection.transmit(apdu)\n    if expect_response:\n        return response, sw1, sw2\n    else:\n        return sw1, sw2\n\ndef select_application(connection, aid):\n    apdu = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x04, 0x00, len(aid)] + aid\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef authenticate_ev2(connection, key_no, key):\n    apdu = [0x00, 0x82, 0x00, key_no, len(key)] + list(key)\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef create_ef_file(connection, fid, size, read_key, write_key):\n    size_bytes = size.to_bytes(2, 'big')\n    data = fid + list(size_bytes) + [read_key, write_key]\n    apdu = [0x90, 0xE0, 0x00, 0x00, len(data)] + data + [0x00]\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu)\n\ndef write_ef_file(connection, fid, offset, data):\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    apdu_write = [0x00, 0xD6, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, len(data)] + list(data)\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_write)\n\ndef read_ef_file(connection, fid, offset, length):\n    apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n    send_apdu(connection, apdu_select)\n    apdu_read = [0x00, 0xB0, (offset >> 8) & 0xFF, offset & 0xFF, length]\n    return send_apdu(connection, apdu_read)\n\nclass TestMifarePlusEV2Personalization(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Mock connection object\n        self.connection = MagicMock()\n        # Default transmit returns (response, sw1, sw2)\n        self.connection.transmit = MagicMock(return_value=([0x01, 0x02, 0x03], 0x90, 0x00))\n\n    def test_select_application_success(self):\n        aid = [0xD2, 0x76, 0x00, 0x00, 0x85, 0x01, 0x01]\n        response, sw1, sw2 = select_application(self.connection, aid)\n        apdu = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x04, 0x00, len(aid)] + aid\n        self.connection.transmit.assert_called_with(apdu)\n        self.assertEqual(response, [0x01, 0x02, 0x03])\n        self.assertEqual(sw1, 0x90)\n        self.assertEqual(sw2, 0x00)\n\n    def test_authenticate_ev2_success(self):\n        key_no = 0x01\n        key = KEYS[key_no]\n        response, sw1, sw2 = authenticate_ev2(self.connection, key_no, key)\n        expected_apdu = [0x00, 0x82, 0x00, key_no, len(key)] + list(key)\n        self.connection.transmit.assert_called_with(expected_apdu)\n        self.assertEqual(sw1, 0x90)\n        self.assertEqual(sw2, 0x00)\n\n    def test_create_ef_file_success(self):\n        ef = EF_FILES[0]\n        response, sw1, sw2 = create_ef_file(self.connection, ef['fid'], ef['size'], ef['read_key'], ef['write_key'])\n        size_bytes = ef['size'].to_bytes(2, 'big')\n        data = ef['fid'] + list(size_bytes) + [ef['read_key'], ef['write_key']]\n        apdu = [0x90, 0xE0, 0x00, 0x00, len(data)] + data + [0x00]\n        self.connection.transmit.assert_called_with(apdu)\n        self.assertEqual(sw1, 0x90)\n        self.assertEqual(sw2, 0x00)\n\n    def test_write_ef_file_success(self):\n        fid = EF_FILES[0]['fid']\n        offset = 0\n        data = b'abcde'\n        # write\n        ]) as mock_send_apdu:\n            response, sw1, sw2 = write_ef_file(self.connection, fid, offset, data)\n            apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n            apdu_write = [0x00, 0xD6, 0x00, 0x00, len(data)] + list(data)\n            calls = [((self.connection, apdu_select),), ((self.connection, apdu_write),)]\n            # Check both calls\n            self.assertEqual(mock_send_apdu.call_args_list[0][0][1], apdu_select)\n            self.assertEqual(mock_send_apdu.call_args_list[1][0][1], apdu_write)\n            self.assertEqual(sw1, 0x90)\n            self.assertEqual(sw2, 0x00)\n\n    def test_read_ef_file_success(self):\n        fid = EF_FILES[0]['fid']\n        offset = 0\n        length = 5\n        with patch(__name__ + '.send_apdu', side_effect=[\n            ([0x00], 0x90, 0x00),  # select\n            ([0x01, 0x02, 0x03, 0x04, 0x05], 0x90, 0x00)  # read\n        ]) as mock_send_apdu:\n            response, sw1, sw2 = read_ef_file(self.connection, fid, offset, length)\n            apdu_select = [0x00, 0xA4, 0x00, 0x00, 0x02] + fid\n            apdu_read = [0x00, 0xB0, 0x00, 0x00, length]\n            self.assertEqual(mock_send_apdu.call_args_list[0][0][1], apdu_select)\n            self.assertEqual(mock_send_apdu.call_args_list[1][0][1], apdu_read)\n            self.assertEqual(response, [0x01, 0x02, 0x03, 0x04, 0x05])\n            self.assertEqual(sw1, 0x90)\n            self.assertEqual(sw2, 0x00)\n\n    def test_create_ef_file_invalid_size(self):\n        #
